          <div id="titlecartoon">
           <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
            <a href="http://vivalesbootlegs.blogspot.com/2015/07/the-specials-paradiso-amsterdam-1980.html">
             The Specials: Paradiso, Amsterdam, 1980. The Paradiso, Amsterdam, The Netherlands - 1980.01.21. (Excellent Soundboard :: Lossless FLAC)
            </a>
           </h3>
          </div>
          <div id="titlecartoonbottom">
          </div>
          <div class="post-header-line-1">
          </div>
          <div class="excerpt post-body entry-content">
           <!-- START FRONT Old artwork code-->
           <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ivbLdmp61Uc/VaGEgWkw5QI/AAAAAAAAH08/_tdsQ5t11do/s1600/specials-paradiso-1980-front_.jpg">
            <img alt=" front cover" border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ivbLdmp61Uc/VaGEgWkw5QI/AAAAAAAAH08/_tdsQ5t11do/s400/specials-paradiso-1980-front_.jpg" style="display: block; margin: 0px auto 10px; text-align: center; width: 400px;"/>
           </a>
           <br/>
           <!-- start BACK artwork front code-->
           <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0PkSedmRw4c/VaGEgvyjtiI/AAAAAAAAH04/0LKf9zwl7RE/s1600/specials-paradiso-1980-back_.jpg">
            <img alt="back cover" border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0PkSedmRw4c/VaGEgvyjtiI/AAAAAAAAH04/0LKf9zwl7RE/s400/specials-paradiso-1980-back_.jpg" style="display: block; margin: 0px auto 10px; text-align: center; width: 400px;"/>
           </a>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            The Specials: Paradiso, Amsterdam, 1980.
           </span>
           <span style="color: #666666; font-size: 78%;">
            (No Label)
           </span>
           <br/>
           Recorded Live at The Paradiso, Amsterdam, The Netherlands - January 21, 1980.
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              Excellent Soundboard recording
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc33;">
              Japanese Pro CD-R
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              Lossless FLAC
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              .
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           01. Dawning Of A New Era
           <br/>
           02. Do The Dog
           <br/>
           03. It's Up To You
           <br/>
           04. Monkey Man
           <br/>
           05. Rat Race
           <br/>
           06. Blank Expression
           <br/>
           07. Rude Boys Outta Jail
           <br/>
           08. Concrete Jungle
           <br/>
           09. Too Hot
           <br/>
           10. Doesn't Make It Alright
           <br/>
           11. Stupid Marriage
           <br/>
           12. Too Much Too Young
           <br/>
           13. Guns Of Navarone
           <br/>
           14. Little Bitch
           <br/>
           15. A Message To You Rudy
           <br/>
           16. Nite Club
           <br/>
           17. Gangsters
           <br/>
           18. Long Shot Kick De Bucket
           <br/>
           19. Liquidator
           <br/>
           20. Skinhead Moonstomp
           <br/>
           21. Madness
           <br/>
           22. You're Wondering Now
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Files:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             22.
            </span>
            <span style="color: #333333;">
             ::
            </span>
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Size:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             473.20 MB (flac).
            </span>
            <br/>
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Total Time:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             01:11:46 hour/s.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <br/>
            <span style="font-size: 85%;">
             *** 1980 European Tour ***
            </span>
           </div>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Notes:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             SBD, Lineage - Silver &gt; EAC (secure) &gt; WAV &gt; TLH &gt; Flac8
             <br/>
             <br/>
             All thanks to the taper. These do not appear to be the recordings used for
             <b>
              'Blue Plate Special'
             </b>
             - they seem to be taken from an audience tape instead, &amp;  appear to be from a different performance - &amp; this show is much more energetic....
            </span>
            .
            <span style="color: #666666; font-style: italic;">
             &lt;
             <span style="color: #999999;">
              info taken from the original .nfo file
             </span>

           </a>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Def Leppard: White Lightning.
           </span>
           <span style="color: #666666; font-size: 78%;">
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%; font-style: italic; font-weight: bold;">
            (
            <span style="color: #33ff33;">
             Not Guilty label
            </span>

            )
           </span>

           Recorded Live at Ancienne Belgique, Brussels, Belgium - May 30, 1992.
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">

             <span style="color: #666666;">

           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Disc 1
           </span>
           <br/>

           <br/>
           02. Tear It Down
           <br/>

           <br/>

           <br/>

             Total Time:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             01:56:22 hour/s.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <span style="font-size: 85%;">
             *** Adrenalize tour ***
            </span>
           </div>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Personnel:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Joe Elliott - Lead Vocals :: Phil Collen - Guitar/Vocals :: Vivian Campbell - Guitar/Vocals :: Rick Savage - Bass/Vocals :: Rick Allen - Drums.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Notes:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             This is one of my favorite live recordings of Def Leppard. This takes place on the 13 Day Club Tour that kicked off the 1992-1993 Adrenalize tour. The quality is great and it's taken from a good old fashioned silver CD bootleg called "White Lightning," issued on the Not Guilty label (NG 170992-2).
             <br/>
             <br/>
             The first show in this city since April 1988 on the Hysteria tour.
             <span style="color: #ffcc33; font-weight: bold;">
              The audience recording of this show is extremely good
             </span>
             . It is sometimes known as 'White Lightning' (Not Guilty NG 170992-2).
             <span style="color: #ffcc33;">
              Once mentioned by Joe as being up there with the 1983 LA Forum recording as his favourite bootleg
             </span>
            </span>
            .
            <span style="color: #666666; font-style: italic;">
             &lt;-(Info taken from deflepparduk.com &amp; original info files)

           <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
            <a href="http://vivalesbootlegs.blogspot.com/2012/04/deep-purple-live-in-japan-complete.html">
             Deep Purple: Live In Japan Complete. Festival Hall, Osaka + Budokan, Tokyo, Japan - 1972.08.15,16,17. (6CD  DTB  lossless FLAC &amp; MP3 @320 Kbps)
            </a>
           </h3>
          </div>
          <div id="titlecartoonbottom">
          </div>
          <div class="post-header-line-1">
          </div>
          <div class="excerpt post-body entry-content">
           <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oEP9wd7iKMc/VZ4mCB0U-5I/AAAAAAAAH0s/R4nhWSY8SFU/s1600/Live%2BIn%2BJapan%2BComplete%2Bfront.jpg">
            <img alt="FRONT" border="0" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5733672452879305330" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oEP9wd7iKMc/VZ4mCB0U-5I/AAAAAAAAH0s/R4nhWSY8SFU/s400/Live%2BIn%2BJapan%2BComplete%2Bfront.jpg" style="cursor: hand; cursor: pointer; display: block; height: 305px; margin: 0px auto 10px; text-align: center; width: 400px;"/>
           </a>
           <br/>
           <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QsYt0NNOxuk/VZ4mB8DtLeI/AAAAAAAAH0o/fWaHVzpoeQs/s1600/Live%2BIn%2BJapan%2BComplete%2Bback.jpg">
            <img alt="BACK" border="0" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5733672459890565922" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QsYt0NNOxuk/VZ4mB8DtLeI/AAAAAAAAH0o/fWaHVzpoeQs/s400/Live%2BIn%2BJapan%2BComplete%2Bback.jpg" style="cursor: hand; cursor: pointer; display: block; height: 305px; margin: 0px auto 10px; text-align: center; width: 400px;"/>
           </a>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Deep Purple: Live In Japan Complete.
           </span>
           <span style="color: #666666; font-size: 78%;">
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%; font-style: italic;">
            (
            <span style="color: #33ff33; font-weight: bold;">
             Darker Than Blue
            </span>
            ::
            <span style="color: #33ff33;">
             Darker Than Blue 044/045/046/047/048/049
            </span>
            )
           </span>
           <br/>
           Recorded Live at Festival Hall + Budokan , Osaka + Tokyo , Japan - August 15, 16 and 17, 1972.
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              Ex-/VG+ Audience Recordings
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc33;">
              Silver CDs
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              MP3 CBR 320 kbps &amp; FLAC
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              .
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Disc 1
           </span>
           <br/>

           <br/>

           <br/>
           03. Child In Time
           <br/>
           04. The Mule
           <br/>

            </span>

             27.
            </span>

             ::

            </span>

             686.75 MB (mp3)
             <span style="color: #666666; font-size: 78%;">
              |
             </span>
             1.67 GB (flac).
            </span>
            <br/>
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Total Time:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             05:00:11 hour/s.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <span style="font-size: 85%;">
             *** First tour of Japan ***
            </span>
           </div>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <br/>
           </div>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Personnel:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Ritchie Blackmore  lead guitar, Ian Gillan  vocals, harmonica, percussion, Roger Glover  bass guitar, Jon Lord  organ, keyboards, electric piano, Ian Paice  drums, percussion.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Notes:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Deep Purples legendary three concerts in Japan on their first visit to the far east were all professionally recorded and have been available for thirty years. The 2LP set Live In Japan, originally for the Japanese market only but gained world-wide release, is considered by some to be the best live album of any band to emerge from the seventies. Released just in time for the Christmas season, it edited together songs from all three nights. In 1993 a more complete, three compact disc version was released which devoted one disc for each show. Given the limitations of space each show is still incomplete. Two tracks, Lazy from the August 17th Tokyo show and Black Night from the August 16th Osaka tape appear on the 2002 six disc release Listen, Learn, Read On. The second track is important since it was previously unreleased.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #ffcc33; font-weight: bold;">
              Live In Japan Complete
             </span>
             collects three good audience recordings and
             <span style="color: #ffcc33;">
              offers the most complete versions of these concerts spread over six cds
             </span>
             . Not all of these sources offer the best sound quality, but they are all listenable. These three dates are the first
             <span style="font-weight: bold;">
              Deep Purple
             </span>
             played in the far east and account for the entire tour. The playing in these shows are one of the highlights of the Mark II line up and are an amazing contrast to their second tour of Japan almost a year later, which would be the last ones with
             <span style="font-weight: bold;">
              Ian Gillan
             </span>
             and
             <span style="font-weight: bold;">
              Roger Glover
             </span>
             . Those concerts would have almost identical set lists but the tension within the band is obvious, especially in the final show in Osaka on June 29th, 1973 and documented on Darker Than Blues
             <span style="font-style: italic; font-weight: bold;">
              The End
             </span>
             (Darker Than Blue 031/32)
            </span>
            .
            <span style="color: #666666; font-style: italic;">
             &lt;-(Info taken from Collectors Music Reviews)
            </span>
            .
           </span>

             Eric Clapton: The Sheriff's Residence. Royal Albert Hall, London, UK - May 23, 2009. (Double CD :: Godfather :: Lossless FLAC)
            </a>
           </h3>
          </div>
          <div id="titlecartoonbottom">
          </div>
          <div class="post-header-line-1">

          <div class="excerpt post-body entry-content">
           <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wAwT8HYBKZU/TXSPB6FHrsI/AAAAAAAAFgI/bH69ildUo6E/s1600/EC%2BThe%2BSheriff%2527s%2BResidence%2Bfront.jpg" onblur="try {parent.deselectBloggerImageGracefully();} catch(e) {}">

           </a>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Eric Clapton: The Sheriff's Residence.
           </span>
           <span style="color: #666666; font-size: 78%;">
            (The Godfatherecords
            <span style="color: #333333;">
             ::
            </span>
            G.R.401/402)
           </span>
           <br/>
           Recorded Live at Royal Albert Hall,  London, UK - May 23, 2009.
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">

             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              Excellent Audience Recording
             </span>

            </span>

             <span style="font-weight: bold;">
              02:02:41
             </span>
             hour/s.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <span style="font-size: 85%;">
             *** Eric Clapton's 2009 UK tour ***
            </span>
           </div>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <br/>
           </div>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Personnel:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Eric Clapton: guitar, vocals
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Andy Fairweather Low: guitar, vocals
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Steve Gadd: drums
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Willy Weeks: bass
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Chris Stainton: Pianos and keys
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Tim Carmon: Hammond and keys
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Michelle John: backing vocals
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Sharon White: backing vocals.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Notes:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Bonus: Everythings Gonna Be All Right (bonus track from May 20 2009 royal albert hall, london)
             <br/>
             <br/>
             The Sheriffs Residence documents the sixth of the eleven shows Clapton played at the Royal Albert Hall.  Godfather use an excellent, clear and dynamic audience tape of the entire show which is up to the same high standards as the other tapes to emerge from this series of shows.  The pattern of the set pretty much remained the same but with minor variations over the various concerts.   Godfather includes as a bonus track Everythings Gonna Be Alright from the May 20th show.  This was played in the set in lieu of Not Dark Yet in about half of the RAH concerts and is included for completeness sake.  The label use several photographs from the show on the inside cover of the gatefold sleeve.  The eleven shows are all documented in great sounding tapes and most of them now are released in excellent silver editions.  The Sheriffs Residence is an impressive Clapton release on Godfather worth having
            </span>
            .

             &lt;-(Info taken from collectorsmusicreviews.com)

             01:35:07 hour/s.
            </span>

           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <span style="font-size: 85%;">
             *** Japan Tour '80 ***
            </span>
           </div>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">

           <span style="font-size: 85%;">

            </span>

             Notes:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             This version is from the Tarantura bootleg version of an audience recording taped by famous Mr Peach. Many thanks to Dime user
             <span style="font-weight: bold;">
              fuwawuwatime
             </span>
             for sending us
             <span style="color: #ffcc33; font-weight: bold;">
              this extremely great recording
             </span>
             ! The sound and mix are VERY clear and strong, very close to a soundboard recording.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             The recording for the late show featured here is clear and very powerful with an excellent well balanced sound and
             <span style="color: #ffcc33; font-weight: bold;">
              could easily be mistaken for a soundboard recording
             </span>
             , it is very similar in tone to the afternoon show and is another Peach masterpiece. You have no real problem picking out the instruments in the recording, there is wonderful separation between the bass and guitar and is a real joy to listen too. The crowd is very quiet and respectful and there is no interference by the taper, obviously they are mesmerized by the band
            </span>
            .

            <span style="font-size: 85%;">
             *** Quadrophenia U.S. Tour 1973 ***
            </span>
           </div>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <br/>
           </div>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Personnel:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Roger Daltrey  lead vocals, harmonica
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Pete Townshend  guitar, vocals
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             John Entwistle  bass guitar, vocals
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Keith Moon  drums.
            </span>

           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Notes:
            </span>
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             2CD-remaster.
            </span>
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             The Who's infamous '73 Cow Palace concert, their first in America in nearly two years.  Despite its reputation as one of the worst gigs the Who ever did (K Moon passes out during WGFA!), the first part of the show including Quadrophenia is quite good, at times exceptional.  This version has been speed corrected and re-tracked from the silvers.
            </span>
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="color: #666666; font-style: italic;">
             &lt;-(Info taken from original info file)
            </span>
            .
           </span>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             <br/>
             An actually decent audience recording that is very much an upgrade from the older Our Drummer's Out Cold (CD) (Wholiday Music WH 008/9) which was a bad dub off the Bill Graham video. You can actually understand the stage announcements and hear the instruments. Decent soundstage and probably taken from close to a first generation  recording.
            </span>
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="color: #666666; font-style: italic;">
             &lt;-(Info taken from
             <span style="color: #ff6600;">
              thewho.net
             </span>
             )
            </span>
            .

             Lineage:

            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             30.

            </span>

             286.77 MB (mp3) / 847 MB (flac).
            </span>

            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Total Time:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             02:05:19 hour/s.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <span style="font-size: 85%;">
             *** Roll the Bones Tour ***
            </span>
           </div>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <br/>
           </div>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Personnel:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Geddy Lee
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Alex Lifeson
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Neil Peart.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Notes:
            </span>
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             (Audio - 9)
            </span>
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             This is the best sounding audience tape ever! It actually sounds so much better than almost every other soundboard out there! I like this bootleg a whole lot more than "Mirrors", most would disagree  with me, but it IS they who are wrong! The performance in "Mirrors" is pretty bad when compared to... well,  lets just say Kenny G packs more raw passion into his shows. At least in my set list, "Mirrors" has just become  obsolete. Never again will I sit through that bland performance. Throughout "Force Ten" you can hear the  audience REALLY talk a lot, then they are in the perfect mix for every single second of the rest of the show! I  think this is a tremendous must have, I cannot think of one single knock on this one, the sound is 100% and the  erformance is above average for a great live band! A funny little thing is Alex is freaking out during "Closer  o the Heart", he usually does his improv and says something that is at least a sentence structure to it.  This time he just spats out things at a hundred miles an hour and I just struggle to keep up, let alone  understand. Perfect show, get this one for sure!. -Review by
             <span style="color: #ff6600;">
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>

           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Blind Faith: Gothenburg 1969.
           </span>
           <span style="color: #666666; font-size: 78%;">
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%; font-style: italic;">
            (
            <span style="color: #33ff33; font-weight: bold;">
             Moby Dick (Swingin' Pig)
            </span>
            ::
            <span style="color: #33ff33;">
             MD CD 003
            </span>
            )
           </span>
           <br/>
           Recorded Live in Gothenburg, Sweden - June 18, 1969.
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              Very Good Audience Recording
             </span>

              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc33;">
              Bootleg Silver CD
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              CBR 320 kbps &amp; FLAC
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              .
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           </span>
           01. Sleeping in the Ground
           <br/>
           02. Sea Of Joy
           <br/>
           03. Under My Thumb
           <br/>
           04. Can't Find My Way Home
           <br/>
           05. Presence of the Lord
           <br/>
           06. Had to Cry Today
           <br/>
           07. Do What You Like
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Files:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             7.
            </span>
            <span style="color: #333333;">
             ::
            </span>
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Size:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             150.07 MB (mp3) / 352 MB (flac).
            </span>
            <br/>
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Total Time:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             01:05:37 hour/s.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Personnel:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Eric Clapton Guitar, Vocals
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Steve Winwood Keyboards, Vocals
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Ginger Baker Drums
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Rick Grech Bass .
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Notes:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Sound quality isn't soundboard standard being an audience recording, but it's perfectly acceptable if slightly distant. The performance is good too though Do What You Like will never be my favourite BF song. The band are relaxed and show what they could have been given a little more time and less pressure to make big bucks. Recommended. - (DR)
            </span>

           <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
            <a href="http://vivalesbootlegs.blogspot.com/2010/10/cream-real-one-detroit-mi-grande.html">

           </h3>
          </div>

          </div>

          </div>

            <img alt="" border="0" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5523513555441193874" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_VIt42ZwDrR4/TKd2UFggk5I/AAAAAAAAERo/g4uaSrilLVs/s400/Cream+The+Real+One+Front.jpg" style="cursor: pointer; display: block; height: 391px; margin: 0px auto 10px; text-align: center; width: 400px;"/>
           </a>
           <br/>
           <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_VIt42ZwDrR4/TKd2T1cOMyI/AAAAAAAAERg/JhoTu1edab8/s1600/Cream+The+Real+One+Back.jpg" onblur="try {parent.deselectBloggerImageGracefully();} catch(e) {}">
            <img alt="" border="0" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5523513551128245026" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_VIt42ZwDrR4/TKd2T1cOMyI/AAAAAAAAERg/JhoTu1edab8/s400/Cream+The+Real+One+Back.jpg" style="cursor: pointer; display: block; height: 315px; margin: 0px auto 10px; text-align: center; width: 400px;"/>
           </a>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Cream: The Real One.
           </span>
           <span style="color: #666666; font-size: 78%;">
            (
            <b>
             <span style="color: lime;">
              Rothmans
             </span>
            </b>
            <span style="color: #333333;">
             ::
            </span>
            <span style="color: lime;">
             RM 009/10
            </span>
            )
           </span>
           <br/>
           Recorded Live at Grande Ballroom, Detroit, Michigan, USA - October 15, 1967.
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              Excellent Soundboard Recording
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc33;">
              Bootleg Silver CD
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">

             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              .
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Disc 1
           </span>
           <br/>
           01. Tales of Brave Ulysses
           <br/>
           02. N.S.U.
           <br/>
           03. Sitting On Top of the World
           <br/>
           04. Sweet Wine
           <br/>
           05. Rollin' And Tumblin'
           <br/>
           06. Spoonful
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Disc 2
           </span>
           <br/>
           01. Steppin' Out
           <br/>
           02. Traintime
           <br/>
           03. Toad
           <br/>
           04. I'm So Glad
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">

             Files:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             10.
            </span>
            <span style="color: #333333;">
             ::
            </span>
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Size:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             <span style="color: #333333;">
             </span>
             668 MB (flac).
            </span>
            <br/>
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Total Time:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             01:54:38 hour
             <span style="font-size: 78%;">
              /
             </span>
             s.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Personnel:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Eric Clapton
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Jack Bruce
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Ginger Baker.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Notes:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             This show in Detroit has turned up on a number of titles including the dodgy Creamset on Gold Standard. It's a very good show rightly regarded by Cream fans as one of the best of the late '67 tour of the US. For its vintage, the recording is very good and you can really hear why Cream had such an impact as a live act. On Sweet Wine and Rollin' and Tumbin' Ginger and Jack really lock together allowing Eric free rein to shine: and shine he does. Highly recommended
            </span>
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             -
             <span style="font-style: italic;">
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ff6600; font-style: italic;">
              DR
             </span>

           <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
            <a href="http://vivalesbootlegs.blogspot.com/2011/07/led-zeppelin-last-concert-in-america.html">
             Led Zeppelin: The Last Concert In America. Alameda County Coliseum, Oakland, California, USA - 1977.07.24. (Double CD :: Tarantura :: Lossless FLAC)
            </a>
           </h3>
          </div>
          <div id="titlecartoonbottom">
          </div>
          <div class="post-header-line-1">
          </div>
          <div class="excerpt post-body entry-content">
           <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-AuL24MO7xM4/ThnfXax3VwI/AAAAAAAAFp0/3U8yBL2064A/s1600/Led%2BZeppelin%2BLast%2BConcert%2BAmerica%2BFront%2Bblog.jpg" onblur="try {parent.deselectBloggerImageGracefully();} catch(e) {}">
            <img alt="" border="0" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5627774802794600194" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-AuL24MO7xM4/ThnfXax3VwI/AAAAAAAAFp0/3U8yBL2064A/s400/Led%2BZeppelin%2BLast%2BConcert%2BAmerica%2BFront%2Bblog.jpg" style="cursor: hand; cursor: pointer; display: block; height: 391px; margin: 0px auto 10px; text-align: center; width: 400px;"/>
           </a>
           <br/>
           <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-TEFji2dQddw/ThnfXjBHmPI/AAAAAAAAFp8/L1OZL_f3-sU/s1600/Led%2BZeppelin%2BLast%2BConcert%2BAmerica%2BBack%2Bblog.jpg" onblur="try {parent.deselectBloggerImageGracefully();} catch(e) {}">
            <img alt="LED ZEPPELIN" border="0" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5627774805006063858" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-TEFji2dQddw/ThnfXjBHmPI/AAAAAAAAFp8/L1OZL_f3-sU/s400/Led%2BZeppelin%2BLast%2BConcert%2BAmerica%2BBack%2Bblog.jpg" style="cursor: hand; cursor: pointer; display: block; height: 377px; margin: 0px auto 10px; text-align: center; width: 400px;"/>
           </a>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Led Zeppelin: The Last Concert In America.
           </span>
           <span style="color: #666666; font-size: 78%;">
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%; font-style: italic; font-weight: bold;">
            (
            <span style="color: #33ff33;">
             Tarantura
            </span>
            ::
            <span style="color: #33ff33;">
             TCD-101-1, 2
            </span>
            )
           </span>
           <br/>
           Recorded Live at Alameda County Coliseum, Oakland, California, USA - July 24, 1977.
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              Very Good Audience Recording
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc33;">
              Silver CDs
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #ffcc00;">
              Lossless FLAC
             </span>
             <span style="color: #666666;">
              .
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Disc 1
           </span>
           <br/>
           01. Opening
           <br/>
           02. The Song Remains The Same
           <br/>
           03. Sick Again
           <br/>
           04. Nobody's Fault But Mine
           <br/>
           05. Over The Hills And Far Away
           <br/>
           06. Since I've Been Loving You
           <br/>
           07. No Quarter
           <br/>
           08. Ten Years Gone
           <br/>
           09. The Battle Of Evermore
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Disc 2
           </span>
           <br/>
           01. Going To California
           <br/>
           02. Mystery Train
           <br/>
           03. Black Country Woman
           <br/>
           04. Bron-Y-Aur Stomp
           <br/>
           05. Trampled Underfoot
           <br/>
           06. White Summer - Black Mountain Side
           <br/>
           07. Kashmir
           <br/>
           08. Jimmy Page Solo
           <br/>
           09. Achilles Last Stand
           <br/>
           10. Stairway To Heaven
           <br/>
           11. Whole Lotta Love
           <br/>
           12. Rock And Roll
           <br/>
           13. Ending MC
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Files:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             22.
            </span>
            <span style="color: #333333;">
             ::
            </span>
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Size:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             639 MB (flac).
            </span>
            <br/>
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Total Time:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             02:38:06 hour/s.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <div style="color: #ff6600; font-weight: bold;">
            <span style="font-size: 85%;">
             *** Led Zeppelin North American Tour 1977 ***
            </span>
           </div>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Personnel:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Jimmy Page
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             John Paul Jones
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             Robert Plant
             <span style="color: #333333;">
              ::
             </span>
             John Bonham.
            </span>
           </span>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="font-weight: bold;">
             Notes:
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             This is a
             <span style="color: #ffcc33;">
              very good audience recording
             </span>
             , meaning one below excellent. A girl does shout PAGE at quite a few moments between songs right into the mic, but that just adds to the atmosphere. Over all, the band is really on this day. There are some mic movements at various parts on CD 2, but nothing that interferes with the music.  It is balanced over all and very listenable, given that its at a stadium with over 67,000 people on who knows what inside. Again, the first few notes of each song are not cut off, but the show is not complete, with missing Whole Lotta Love.
             <br/>
             <br/>
            </span>
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             Tarantura has done an excellent job with editing
            </span>
           </span>
           <span style="font-size: 85%;">
            <span style="color: #999999;">
             that did have to be done, and with EQing. This is now the definitive release for Led Zepps last concert.
             <span style="color: #999999;">
              Highly recommended
             </span>
            </span>
            .
            <span style="color: #666666; font-style: italic;">
             (Info taken from
             <b>
              <span style="color: #3d85c6;">
               collectorsmusicreviews
              </span>
             </b>
             )
            </span>
            .
           </span>

           * * * * * * *
          </p>
          <p class="textbootsinfo">
           <em>
            From Wikipedia:
           </em>
           <br/>
           Bootlegging is often incorrectly referred to as piracy but there are important differences between the two terms. Non-profit bootlegging is trafficking in
           <strong>
            recordings that the record companies have not commercially released
           </strong>
           , whereas piracy is the illegal copying/sale of recordings that are available commercially.
          </p>

       <div class="widget HTML" id="HTML2">
        <h2 class="title">
         Bootlegging
        </h2>
        <div class="widget-content">
         Bootlegging is often incorrectly referred to as piracy but there are important differences between the two terms. Non-profit bootlegging is trafficking in recordings that the record companies have not commercially released, whereas piracy is the illegal copying/sale of recordings that are (or have been) available commercially or are planned/scheduled for commercial release.
        </div>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <span class="widget-item-control">
         <span class="item-control blog-admin">
          <a class="quickedit" href="//www.blogger.com/rearrange?blogID=8011549648749498349&amp;widgetType=HTML&amp;widgetId=HTML2&amp;action=editWidget&amp;sectionId=col5" onclick='return _WidgetManager._PopupConfig(document.getElementById("HTML2"));' target="configHTML2" title="Modifier">
           <img alt="" height="18" src="//img1.blogblog.com/img/icon18_wrench_allbkg.png" width="18"/>
          </a>
         </span>
        </span>

     <p>
      This blog is merely an  index with public links for audio recordings of independent origin (ROIO) which have not been officially released. No audio or video content is hosted here. We only provide meta information files for the ROIOs.	
If you're an artist (or a legal representative of an artist or its estate) and you don't want your ROIOs shared on this blog
      <strong>
       <em>
        for FREE
       </em>
      </strong>
      among your fans, you may opt out any time by sending
      <a href="mailto:viva.lbs+contact@gmail.com">
       e-mail
      </a>
      to the site admin. We will then put you in our list of not allowed artists. This will halt all sharing of your ROIOs in this blog within minutes.	
BTW, the ROIOs exist, you can't make them vanish. So, why not let your fans get them for free from one another instead of
      <strong>
       having to purchase them from commercial bootleggers on auction sites
      </strong>
      ?
